                        "import os\nimport shutil\nimport tempfile\nimport unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, mock_open, MagicMock, call\nimport builtins\n\n# Import the functions to test\n# Since the code is not in a module, we'll assume the code is pasted above this test script in the same file.\n# If in a module, e.g. vhdl_automation.py, you would do:\n# from vhdl_automation import (\n#     tidy_vhdl_files, document_vhdl_files, write_vhdl_module,\n#     run_vhdl_simulation, hardware_verification, synthesize_and_build,\n#     run_scripted_tests, git_commit_push, run_cmd, log\n# )\n\n# For this test script, we will redefine the constants as the tested code expects them to be globals.\n# We'll patch them in setUp/tearDown as needed.\n\nimport sys\n\n# Patch the global variables in the tested code's namespace\nimport types\n\n# Assume the tested code is in the current namespace (since it's a script)\ntested_globals = globals()\n\nclass TestVHDLAutomation(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create temp dirs for VHDL, testbenches, etc.\n        self.test_dir = tempfile.TemporaryDirectory()\n        self.vhdl_dir = os.path.join(self.test_dir.name, \"vhdl\")\n        self.tb_dir = os.path.join(self.test_dir.name, \"testbenches\")\n        self.vivado_proj_dir = os.path.join(self.test_dir.name, \"fpga_proj\")\n        self.bitstream_dir = os.path.join(self.test_dir.name, \"bitstreams\")\n        self.git_repo_dir = os.path.join(self.test_dir.name, \"repo\")\n        os.makedirs(self.vhdl_dir)\n        os.makedirs(self.tb_dir)\n        os.makedirs(self.vivado_proj_dir)\n        os.makedirs(self.bitstream_dir)\n        os.makedirs(self.git_repo_dir)\n\n        # Patch the global variables in the tested code\n        tested_globals['VHDL_DIR'] = self.vhdl_dir\n        tested_globals['TB_DIR'] = self.tb_dir\n        tested_globals['VIVADO_PROJ_DIR'] = self.vivado_proj_dir\n        tested_globals['BITSTREAM_DIR'] = self.bitstream_dir\n        tested_globals['GIT_REPO_DIR'] = self.git_repo_dir\n        tested_globals['LOG_FILE'] = os.path.join(self.test_dir.name, \"automation.log\")\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        self.test_dir.cleanup()\n\n    def test_tidy_vhdl_files_basic_and_edge(self):\n        # Create a VHDL file with tabs, trailing spaces, and a non-VHDL file\n        vhdl_file = os.path.join(self.vhdl_dir, \"test1.vhd\")\n        with open(vhdl_file, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(\"entity test is\\n\\tport(\\n\\tclk : in std_logic   \\n\\t);\\nend;\\n\")\n        non_vhdl_file = os.path.join(self.vhdl_dir, \"notvhdl.txt\")\n        with open(non_vhdl_file, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(\"Should not be changed\\n\")\n\n        tested_globals['tidy_vhdl_files']()\n        with open(vhdl_file, \"r\") as f:\n            lines = f.readlines()\n        # All lines should have no trailing whitespace and tabs replaced with 4 spaces\n        self.assertTrue(all('\\t' not in line for line in lines))\n        self.assertIn(\"    clk : in std_logic\", lines[2])\n        # Non-VHDL file unchanged\n        with open(non_vhdl_file, \"r\") as f:\n            self.assertEqual(f.read(), \"Should not be changed\\n\")\n\n    def test_document_vhdl_files_adds_header(self):\n        # VHDL file with no header\n        vhdl_file = os.path.join(self.vhdl_dir, \"mod.vhd\")\n        with open(vhdl_file, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(\"entity mod is\\nend;\\n\")\n        # VHDL file with header already\n        vhdl_file2 = os.path.join(self.vhdl_dir, \"mod2.vhd\")\n        with open(vhdl_file2, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(\"-- This is a header\\nentity mod2 is\\nend;\\n\")\n        tested_globals['document_vhdl_files']()\n        with open(vhdl_file, \"r\") as f:\n            content = f.read()\n        self.assertTrue(content.lstrip().startswith(\"--\"))\n        self.assertIn(\"Module: mod.vhd\", content)\n        # For this notebook, we'll redefine them here.\n# In a real test file, you would use:\n# from vhdl_automation import (tidy_vhdl_files, document_vhdl_files, write_vhdl_module,\n#   run_vhdl_simulation, \"./fpga_proj\"\nBITSTREAM_DIR = \"./bitstreams\"\nGIT_REPO_DIR = \".\"\nLOG_FILE = \"automation.log\"\n\ndef log(msg):\n    \"\"\"Log messages to file and print to console.\"\"\"\n    with open(LOG_FILE, \"a\") as f:\n        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\")\n        f.write(f\"[{timestamp}] {msg}\\n\")\n    print(f\"[LOG] {msg}\")\n\ndef run_cmd(cmd, cwd=None):\n    \"\"\"Run a shell command and return output, logging errors.\"\"\"\n    log(f\"Running command: {cmd}\")\n    try:\n        result = subprocess.run(cmd, shell=True, cwd=cwd, check=True,\n                               stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True)\n        log(result.stdout)\n        return result.stdout\n    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n        log(f\"Error: {e.stderr}\")\n        raise\n\ndef tidy_vhdl_files():\n    \"\"\"\n    Tidy up VHDL files using 'vhdl-style' conventions.\n    (For demonstration, we'll just ensure consistent indentation.)\n    \"\"\"\n    for fname in os.listdir(VHDL_DIR):\n        if fname.endswith(\".vhd\"):\n            fpath = os.path.join(VHDL_DIR, fname)\n            log(f\"Tidying VHDL file: {fname}\")\n            with open(fpath, \"r\") as f:\n                lines = f.readlines()\n            # Remove trailing whitespace and ensure 4-space indentation\n            tidied = []\n            for line in lines:\n                tidied.append(line.rstrip().replace(\"\\t\", \"    \"))\n            with open(fpath, \"w\") as f:\n content.lstrip().startswith(\"--\"):\n                log(f\"Adding documentation header to {fname}\")\n                header = (\n                    \"-- =========================================================\\n\"\n                    f\"-- Module: {fname}\\n\"\n                    \"-- Description: [Add description here]\\n\"\n                    \"-- Author: [Your Name]\\n\"\n                    f\"-- Date: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}\\n\"\n                    \"-- =========================================================\\n\"\n                )\n                with open(fpath, \"w\") as f:\n                    f.write(header + content)\n\ndef write_vhdl_module(module_name, entity_ports, architecture_body):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create a new VHDL module with documentation.\n    Args:\n        module_name: Name of the module/entity.\n        entity_ports: List of tuples (name, direction, type).\n        architecture_body: String containing architecture code.\n    \"\"\"\n    fname = f\"{module_name}.vhd\"\n    fpath = os.path.join(VHDL_DIR, fname)\n    log(f\"Writing new VHDL module: {fname}\")\n    header = (\n        \"-- =========================================================\\n\"\n        f\"-- Module: {fname}\\n\"\n        \"-- Description: [Add description here]\\n\"\n        \"-- Author: [Your Name]\\n\"\n [f\"{name} : {direction} {vtype}\" for name, direction, vtype in entity_ports]\n    )\n    entity = (\n        f\"entity {module_name} is\\n\"\n        \"  port (\\n\"\n        f\"    {entity_ports_str}\\n\"\n        \"  );\\n\"\n        \"end entity;\\n\"\n    )\n    architecture = (\n        f\"architecture rtl of {module_name} is\\n\"\n        \"begin\\n\"\n -----------\n\ndef log(msg):\n    \"\"\"Log messages to file and print to console.\"\"\"\n    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\")\n    with open(LOG_FILE, \"a\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"[{timestamp}] {msg}\\n\")\n    print(f\"[LOG] {msg}\")\n\ndef run_cmd(cmd, cwd=None, check=True):\n    \"\"\"\n    Run a shell command and return output, logging errors.\n    Args:\n        cmd (str): Command to run.\n        cwd (str): Working directory.\n        check (bool): If True, raise error on failure.\n    Returns:\n        str: Standard output from command.\n    \"\"\"\n    log(f\"Running command: {cmd}\")\n    try:\n        result = subprocess.run(\n            cmd, shell=True, cwd=cwd, check=check,\n            stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True\n        )\n        if result.stdout:\n            log(result.stdout)\n        if result.stderr:\n            log(result.stderr)\n        return result.stdout\n    except exists.\"\"\"\n    if not os.path.exists(path):\n        os.makedirs(path)\n        log(f\"Created directory: {path}\")\n\n# ----------- VHDL MODULE MANAGEMENT -----------\n\ndef tidy_vhdl_files():\n cmd (str): Command to run.\n        cwd (str): Working directory.\n        check (bool): If True, raise error on failure.\n    Returns:\n        str: Standard output from command.\n    \"\"\"\n
